class=\"sidebar2-title\">htxt.africa is...</h3><div class=\"clear\"></div>\n  <div id=\"faq-jobs\">\n        \n    <div class=\"accordionButton\">Privacy policy &amp; cookies</div>\n    <div class=\"accordionContent\"><p>Some important things you should know about this site.</p>\n<ul>\n<li><del></del>We do use third party cookies on this site – most notably from Google – primarily for the purposes of advertising. The neat thing about these are that you can opt out yourself over at Google’s HQ, if you read through these pages on the <a href=\"https://support.google.com/adsense/answer/answer.py?answer=2839090\">DoubleClick cookie</a> in particular. Other advertising partners (such as <a href=\"http://www.adclickafrica.com\" target=\"_blank\">AdClick Africa</a>) may also drop a cookie on your machine. We also use an analytics cookie from Google.</li>\n<li>Like all web servers, your IP address is logged when you visit <a href=\"http://www.htxt.co.za\" target=\"_blank\">htxt</a>.africa in order that we can track traffic, but we don’t share these with anyone, ever.</li>\n<li>Email addresses collected for our daily newsletter, competition entries or discussion accounts are stored purely for that purpose and kept in a POPI compliant manner. We will never share or sell these on, except in the rare incidence of a competition in which our promo partner insists on getting access to entries. In this case, it will be made very clear in the T&amp;Cs for that compo that this will happen.</li>\n<li>You should probably check this notice at regular intervals as it’s likely to be updated soon.</li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n        \n    <div class=\"accordionButton\">Complaints and corrections</div>\n    <div class=\"accordionContent\"><p>Unlike many news sites, we don’t necessarily proclaim that our reporting will always be unbiased, although we do maintain that most of the time it is. We do, however, take every effort to ensure that our reporting is accurate and fair to all sides in a story.</p>\n<p>If you would like to contact us regarding a story which you feel is incorrect, unrepresentative or out and out defamatory, please contact us using the email address <a href=\"mailto://info@htxt.co.za\" target=\"_blank\">info@htxt.co.za</a>. We’re happy to discuss story details with you and, where appropriate, publish valid corrections as soon as possible.</p>\n</div>\n        \n    <div class=\"accordionButton\">Who makes htxt.africa?</div>\n    <div class=\"accordionContent\"><p>Our writers’ bios are all <span style=\"color: #f37021;\"><a href=\"http://www.htxt.co.za/htxt-africa-is/\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"color: #f37021;\">over here</span></a></span>. It’s a team of rather unparalleled experience and enthusiasm in every field.</p>\n</div>\n        \n    <div class=\"accordionButton\">Get in touch</div>\n    <div class=\"accordionContent\"><p>Our contact form is over here, but if you prefer to do things the old fashioned way, you can <span style=\"color: #f37021;\"><a href=\"mailto:adam@hypertext.co.za\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"color: #f37021;\">email us here</span></a></span>, or even write to us at:</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #f37021;\"><a href=\"http://www.htxt.co.za\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"color: #f37021;\">htxt</span></a></span>.africa<br>\nHypertext Media<br>\n102 on 11th Avenue<br>\nHighlands North<br>\n2192<br>\nJohannesburg<br>\nSouth Africa</p>\n<p>And if you’re really old school, call us on <span style=\"color: #f37021;\">011 023 8005</span>.</p>\n</div>\n        \n    <div class=\"accordionButton\">Got a story tip?</div>\n    <div class=\"accordionContent\"><p>You can contact us <a href=\"http://www.htxt.co.za/contact-htxt-africa/\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"color: #f37021;\">via this form</span></a>, and we’ll be updating with PGP and secure details soon.</p>\n</div>\n        \n    <div class=\"accordionButton\">About htxt.africa</div>\n    <div class=\"accordionContent\"><p><span style=\"color: #f37021;\"><a href=\"http://www.htxt.co.za\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"color: #f37021;\">htxt</span></a></span>.africa is South Africa’s newest and most exciting tech blog, covering everything from the top end of government IT investment and spending down to maker culture, hackspaces and – well, generally – fun. We cover far more of the latter than the former, in fact, and aim to make this the number one community for genuinely interesting stuff that’s coming from South Africa and the rest of the continent.<br>\n<br>\nWe love games, 3D printers, start-ups and innovative apps that will save the world. We believe that all across the continent, tech is making a difference to people’s lives in ways that are revolutionising living and working. htxt.africa was born of the absolute certainty that there’s a tremendous amount of stuff that’s going on, and no-one is covering this stuff with the care, attention and enthusiasm that it deserves.<br>\n<br>\nYou can read all about us <a href=\"http://www.htxt.co.za/contact-htxt-africa/\" target=\"_blank\">over here</a>.</p>\n</div>\n    \n  <div class=\"clear\"></div>   \n  </div> \n\n</div> \n\n\n\n\n<div class=\"widget
